INPUT INSTRUCTIONS

  DATA:
  FILE = dat_pa.dat;

  VARIABLE:
  NAMES   = id day N C sq m1-m20;
  CLUSTER = id;
  USEVAR  = s y1-y20;
  MISSING = .;
  LAGGED  = y20(1) s(1);

  DEFINE:
  s = sq / 10;
  y1 = m1 / 10;
  y2 = m2 / 10;
  y3 = m3 / 10;
  y4 = m4 / 10;
  y5 = m5 / 10;
  y6 = m6 / 10;
  y7 = m7 / 10;
  y8 = m8 / 10;
  y9 = m9 / 10;
  y10 = m10 / 10;
  y11 = m11 / 10;
  y12 = m12 / 10;
  y13 = m13 / 10;
  y14 = m14 / 10;
  y15 = m15 / 10;
  y16 = m16 / 10;
  y17 = m17 / 10;
  y18 = m18 / 10;
  y19 = m19 / 10;
  y20 = m20 / 10;

  ANALYSIS:
  TYPE = TWOLEVEL RANDOM;
  ESTIMATOR = BAYES;
  PROC = 8;
  FBITER = 50000;
  BSEED = 1213;

  MODEL:
  %WITHIN%
  y1 (resvar_1);
  y2-y19 (resvar);
  y20 (resvar_2);

  y2-y20 PON y1-y19 (day_ar);

  y1 ON y20&1 (night_ar);
  y1 ON s (beta_y);
  y20 ON s (delta_y);
  s ON y20&1 (beta_s);
  s ON s&1 (ar_s);
  s (resvar_s);

  %BETWEEN%
  mu BY y1-y20@1;
  mu;
  [mu];
  [y1-y20@0];
  y1-y20@0;

  mu s WITH mu s;

  MODEL CONSTRAINT:
  NEW(indirect);
  indirect = beta_y * beta_s;

  OUTPUT:
  TECH1 TECH8 STDYX FSCOMPARISON STAND(CLUSTER);

  PLOT:
  TYPE = PLOT3;
  FACTOR = ALL (500);

  SAVEDATA:
  FILE IS pa_sleep_step1.dat;
  SAVE IS FSCORES (500);
